Disadvantages: The fabric sofa and reclining chairs in the room are too dirty. Of course, it‚Äôs not a problem of cleaning. It‚Äôs old. The surface that can be wiped is very clean. Everyone's service awareness is quite good, just keep it up. .
Others: Mineral water in the room is free, you can ask the front desk if you need it, the robot delivery is very fun, and it is not convenient to take the child to take a bath, just ask the front desk for a bathtub cover, it is not too convenient. . .

Well, the price has been rising these days. If I have a chance to go to Tianjin again, I will stay here again. . .
